(noscript) --><p>A\xc2\xa0<b>kill</b> is the event of decreasing an enemy\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Champion" title="Champion">champion\'s</a>\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Health" title="Health">health</a>\xc2\xa0to zero while the enemy has no\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Champion_ability" title="Champion ability">abilities</a>\xc2\xa0or <a href="/wiki/Item" title="Item">Items</a> to prevent\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a>. Death may be prevented by certain effects, such as those granted by the item\xc2\xa0<span class="inline-image label-after item-icon" data-param="Guardian Angel" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;"><span data-width="20" class="border icon-20" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;"><a href="/wiki/Guardian_Angel" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Guardian Angel" \t \t><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/f/f4/Guardian_Angel_item.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20171221184244" \t alt="Guardian Angel item" \tclass="thumbborder href="/wiki/Zac#Cell_Division" title="Zac">Cell Division</a></span></span></span>.\n</p>\n<nav id="toc" class="toc" data-loaded="false"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rewards"> Rewards </span></h2>\n<p>The last player to strike the target champion is awarded with the kill, and all contributors within the last 10 seconds are awarded with an\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Assist" title="Assist">assist</a>.\n</p><p>When a champion is killed, all players who contributed to the kill receives <a href="/wiki/Gold" title="Gold">gold</a> and <a href="/wiki/Experience_(champion)" title="Experience (champion)">Experience (champion)</a>. Additionally, the player who is awarded with the kill may receive <a href="/wiki/Buff" title="Buff">buffs</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gold_Reward"> Gold Reward </span></h3>\n<p>When a champion is killed, the <strong class="selflink">killer</strong> gets a certain amount of <span class="inline-image label-after" data-param="" style="display:inline;color:gold;white-space:pre;"><span data-width="20" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;"><a href="/wiki/Gold" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Gold" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Gold" \tclass="lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Gold.png" \tdata-image-name="Gold.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/1/10/Gold.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20181122055358" \t width="20" \t height="15" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/1/10/Gold.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20181122055358" \t alt="Gold" \tclass="" \t \tdata-image-key="Gold.png" \tdata-image-name="Gold.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="15" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a></span> <span style="white-space:normal;">Gold</span></span>, while a reduced amount is shared between all the champions that assisted the kill. See <a href="/wiki/Kill#Bounties" title="Kill">bounty</a> for additional info.\nA champion with many consecutive deaths will award a significantly reduced bounty, while one with many consecutive kills will award a higher bounty (refer to Bounty values Notes below for details).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Buff_Reward"> Buff Reward </span></h3>\n<p>If the champion killed has any transferable\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Buff" title="Buff">buffs</a> (<span class="inline-image label-after buff-icon" data-param="Crest of Insight" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;"><span data-width="20" class="border icon-20" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;"><a href="/wiki/Crest_of_Insight" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Crest of Insight" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Crest of Insight buff" \tclass="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Crest_of_Insight_buff.png" \tdata-image-name="Crest of Insight buff.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/6/6f/Crest_of_Insight_buff.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20191119112549" \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/6/6f/Crest_of_Insight_buff.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20191119112549" \t alt="Crest of Insight buff" \tclass="thumbborder " \t \tdata-image-key="Crest_of_Insight_buff.png" \tdata-image-name="Crest of Insight buff.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Crest_of_Insight" title="Crest of Insight">Crest of Insight</a></span></span>\xc2\xa0or\xc2\xa0<span class="inline-image label-after buff-icon" data-param="Crest of Cinders" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;"><span data-width="20" class="border icon-20" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;"><a href="/wiki/Crest_of_Cinders" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Crest of Cinders" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Crest of Cinders buff" \tclass="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Crest_of_Cinders_buff.png" \tdata-image-name="Crest of Cinders buff.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/0/07/Crest_of_Cinders_buff.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20191119112522" \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/0/07/Crest_of_Cinders_buff.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20191119112522" \t alt="Crest of Cinders buff" \tclass="thumbborder " \t \tdata-image-key="Crest_of_Cinders_buff.png" \tdata-image-name="Crest of Cinders buff.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Crest_of_Cinders" title="Crest of Cinders">Crest of Cinders</a></span></span>), the killer champion gains all of these buffs and the duration of each buff is reset.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Execution"> Execution </span></h2>\n<p>If a champion dies and hasn\'t been damaged or debuffed by another champion in the last 13 seconds, they are\xc2\xa0<b>executed</b>. Otherwise, the kill is awarded to the enemy champion who last dealt damage. Executions are caused by a\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Turret" title="Turret">turret</a>,\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Minion" title="Minion">minion</a>, or\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Monster" title="Monster">monster</a>. An execution offers no gold but still grants experience to nearby champions on the opposite team when it is caused by a\xc2\xa0<a href="/wiki/Turret" title="Turret">turret</a> or <a href="/wiki/Minion" title="Minion">minion</a>.\n</p><p>In some cases it could be strategically advantageous for a player to purposefully be executed as an alternative to dying from an enemy champion; in doing so, the enemy receives no gold. Doing this on <a href="/wiki/ARAM" title="ARAM">ARAM</a> allows you to visit the shop without granting kills to the enemy team.\n</p><p>Note that executions do not count as deaths for the purposes of resetting bounties, death streaks or kill streaks.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Execute">Execute</span></h2>\n<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 103px"> \t<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/2/2a/9999_Damage_Execute.png/revision/latest?cb=20200101233840" \tclass="image image-thumbnail" \t \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="9999 Damage Execute" \tclass="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="9999_Damage_Execute.png" \tdata-image-name="9999 Damage Execute.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/2/2a/9999_Damage_Execute.png/revision/latest?cb=20200101233840" \t width="103" \t height="35" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/2/2a/9999_Damage_Execute.png/revision/latest?cb=20200101233840" \t alt="9999 Damage Execute" \tclass="thumbimage " \t \tdata-image-key="9999_Damage_Execute.png" \tdata-image-name="9999 Damage Execute.png" \t \t width="103" \t height="35" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a> \t<figcaption> \t\t \t\t\t<a href="/wiki/File:9999_Damage_Execute.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> \t\t \t\t \t\t \t\t\t<p class="caption"><b>Damage indicator</b></p> \t\t \t</figcaption> </figure>\n<p>An execute is the process of killing a champion at extreme amounts of <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-param="True damage"><a href="/wiki/True_damage" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="True damage" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Hybrid penetration" \tclass="lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Hybrid_penetration.png" \tdata-image-name="Hybrid penetration.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/9/92/Hybrid_penetration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20170514081634" \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/9/92/Hybrid_penetration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20170514081634" \t alt="Hybrid penetration" \tclass="" \t \tdata-image-key="Hybrid_penetration.png" \tdata-image-name="Hybrid penetration.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/True_damage" title="True damage">true damage</a></span>, which is otherwise classified as <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-param="Raw damage"><a href="/wiki/Damage" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Damage" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Fear Beyond Death 2" \tclass="lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Fear_Beyond_Death_2.png" \tdata-image-name="Fear Beyond Death 2.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/4/44/Fear_Beyond_Death_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20171221051936" \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/4/44/Fear_Beyond_Death_2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20171221051936" \t alt="Fear Beyond Death 2" \tclass="" \t \tdata-image-key="Fear_Beyond_Death_2.png" \tdata-image-name="Fear Beyond Death 2.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Damage" title="Damage">raw damage</a></span>. It usually occurs\xc2\xa0if the target is below a certain <span style="color:#C03300;">health</span>\xc2\xa0threshold which does not consider <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-param="Shield"><a href="/wiki/Shield" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Shield" \t \t><img \tdata-image-name="Hybrid resistances icon.png" \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/5/55/Hybrid_resistances_icon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20170516021237" \t alt="Hybrid resistances icon" \tclass="" \t \tdata-image-key="Hybrid_resistances_icon.png" \tdata-image-name="Hybrid resistances icon.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Shield" title="Shield">shields</a></span>.\nTake note that <a href="/wiki/Champion_ability" title="Champion ability">abilities</a> functioning similarly to executes such as <span id="Multi-kill"> Multi-kill </span></h2>\n<p>The act of killing several champions within 10 seconds of each other (30 seconds to Penta Kill after a Quadra Kill if no enemy respawns). The following comments are shown: "Summoner" has slain "(slain name) Summoner" for a [...]!\'\n</p>\n<ul><li> Double Kill (2)\n</li><li> Triple Kill (3)\n</li><li> Quadra Kill (4)\n</li><li> Penta Kill (5)\n</li><li> <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Only on Hexakill mode">Hexa Kill (6)</span>\n</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="History"> History </span></h3>\n<p>Some footage from before the time where <a href="/wiki/Hexakill" title="Hexakill">Hexakill</a> was introduced shows the possibility of getting a <i>Legendary Kill</i>, which can only occur after killing another enemy after a Penta Kill on <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-param="Hexakill"><a href="/wiki/Hexakill" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="Hexakill" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Pentakill II profileicon" \tclass="lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Pentakill_II_profileicon.png" \tdata-image-name="Pentakill II profileicon.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/e/ea/Pentakill_II_profileicon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20170801201912" \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/e/ea/Pentakill_II_profileicon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20170801201912" \t alt="Pentakill II profileicon" \tclass="" \t \tdata-image-key="Pentakill_II_profileicon.png" \tdata-image-name="Pentakill II profileicon.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="20" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Hexakill" title="Hexakill">Hexakill</a></span>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ace"> Ace </span></h2>\n<p>An ace is defined as killing the last living champion of the enemy team. Scoring an ace is far easier than scoring a pentakill, since the only requisite is for the entire allied team to kill the enemy team, rather than one person killing the entire enemy team. There is no gold bonus associated with aces.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bounties"> Bounties </span></h2>\n<p>Teams earn gold rewards when they kill enemy champions. This reward is the bounty of the killed champion. The bounty of a champion depends on his number of consecutive kills or deaths. The number of consecutive kills a champion has is the number of times he has killed enemy champions since he last died or since the match began. The number of consecutive deaths a champion has is the number of times he has died since he last killed an enemy champion or since the match began. The more consecutive kills a champion has, the bigger his bounty. The more consecutive deaths a champion has, the smaller his bounty.\n</p><p>Bounties are divided into two parts:\n</p>\n<ul><li> Kill bounty: Earned by the champion who deals the killing blow.\n</li><li> Assist bounty: Shared evenly among the champions who assist in the kill.\n</li></ul>\n<p>Each part of the bounty is calculated using a system of tiers numbered from -9 to 8. Kill bounties in higher tiers are bigger.\nEach champion starts the match in the bounty tier 0 and moves to other tiers as he kills enemies or dies. Consecutive kills move a champion to a higher tier, while consecutive deaths move him to a lower tier.\n</p><p>This table shows the number of consecutive kills or deaths required to access each tier, and the bounty earned by killing a champion in that tier:\n</p>\n<table class="article-table">\n<tr>\n<th>Tier\n</th><th>Consecutive kills\n</th><th>Consecutive deaths\n</th><th>Kill bounty\n</th><th>Assist bounty\n</th><th>In game announcement\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>8\n</td><td>8+\n</td><td>\n</td><td><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted gray;cursor:help;" title="Capped at 3600 gold</span></span>, plus another <span class="inline-image label-after" data-param="" style="display:inline;color:gold;white-space:pre;"><span data-width="20" gold</span></span> their advantage grows by thereafter. The amount is dynamic and is reduced if the player loses the advantage.\n<ul><li> <b>Average</b> is determined by dividing the enemy team\'s CS gold by 4.<small>3</small>, rather than five, based on the four sources of income on Summoner\'s Rift (top/mid/bot/jungle) + support item income. Modes with smaller teams divide by the number of champs per team instead (ex. 3 for Twisted Treeline).\n</li></ul>\n</li><li> If you die with less CS gold than the enemy team\'s average, you\'ll respawn with a buffer equal to the difference. You won\'t start accruing a CS gold bounty until you\'ve used up the buffer.\n</li><li> All bounties, excluding base bounty, of a team are reduced by 20% if their total team gold is 3% lower than the opposing team\'s gold. The reduction is increased to <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help; color: inherit;" data-size="21" data-values="20 to 40\xe2\x98\x823 to 8" data-label1="Team Gold Deficit" data-displayformula="20%+1% per 0.25% team gold deficit, starting after 3% team gold deficit" data-key1="%" data-key2="%" data-start2="20" data-end2="40" data-values1="\xe2\x98\x823\xe2\x98\x823.25\xe2\x98\x823.5\xe2\x98\x823.75\xe2\x98\x824\xe2\x98\x824.25\xe2\x98\x824.5\xe2\x98\x824.75\xe2\x98\x825\xe2\x98\x825.25\xe2\x98\x825.5\xe2\x98\x825.75\xe2\x98\x826\xe2\x98\x826.25\xe2\x98\x826.5\xe2\x98\x826.75\xe2\x98\x827\xe2\x98\x827.25\xe2\x98\x827.5\xe2\x98\x827.75\xe2\x98\x828" data-values2="\xe2\x98\x8220\xe2\x98\x8221\xe2\x98\x8222\xe2\x98\x8223\xe2\x98\x8224\xe2\x98\x8225\xe2\x98\x8226\xe2\x98\x8227\xe2\x98\x8228\xe2\x98\x8229\xe2\x98\x8230\xe2\x98\x8231\xe2\x98\x8232\xe2\x98\x8233\xe2\x98\x8234\xe2\x98\x8235\xe2\x98\x8236\xe2\x98\x8237\xe2\x98\x8238\xe2\x98\x8239\xe2\x98\x8240">20%&#160;&#8722;&#160;40%&#160;(based on Team Gold Deficit)</span> and further increased to <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; border-bottom:1px dotted; cursor:help; color: inherit;" data-size="13" data-values="" data-label1="Game Time (seconds)" data-displayformula="Starts at 50% and increases by 0.416% per second after minute 1:30 up to minute 3:30" data-key2="%" data-values1="\xe2\x98\x820\xe2\x98\x8290\xe2\x98\x82102\xe2\x98\x82114\xe2\x98\x82126\xe2\x98\x82138\xe2\x98\x82150\xe2\x98\x82162\xe2\x98\x82174\xe2\x98\x82186\xe2\x98\x82198\xe2\x98\x82210\xe2\x98\x82\xe2\x88\x9e" data-values2="\xe2\x98\x8250\xe2\x98\x8250\xe2\x98\x8255\xe2\x98\x8260\xe2\x98\x8265\xe2\x98\x8270\xe2\x98\x8275\xe2\x98\x8280\xe2\x98\x8285\xe2\x98\x8290\xe2\x98\x8295\xe2\x98\x82100\xe2\x98\x82100">50%&#160;&#8722;&#160;100%&#160;(based on Game Time)</span>.\n</li><li> Bounties do not increase mid-combat. If a champion earns multiple kills and then immediately dies, those kills will count toward their next death instead.\n</li><li> A single kill cannot grant more than <span class="inline-image label-after" data-param="" style="display:inline;color:gold;white-space:pre;"><span data-width="20" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;"><a href="/wiki/Gold" \tclass="image image-thumbnail link-internal" \t title="1000 total gold Gold" \t \t><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" \t alt="Gold" \tclass="lzy lzyPlcHld " \t \tdata-image-key="Gold.png" \tdata-image-name="Gold.png" \t data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/1/10/Gold.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20181122055358" \t width="20" \t height="15" \t \t \t onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}" \t><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/leagueoflegends/images/1/10/Gold.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20181122055358" \t alt="Gold" \tclass="" \t \tdata-image-key="Gold.png" \tdata-image-name="Gold.png" \t \t width="20" \t height="15" \t \t \t \t></noscript></a></span> <span style="white-space:normal;">1000 <b>total</b> gold</span></span> to the killer.\n<ul><li> Since a champion\'s bounty can stack to greater values, any remaining gold will carry over. Because of this, enemies can be \'Shutdown\' multiple times in succession.\n</li></ul>\n</li><li> Bounties over <span class="inline-image label-after" data-param="" deficit) are visible in the scoreboard to both allies and enemies.\n</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Triggering_effects_with_kills"> Triggering effects with kills
